JAP_intervene_in_china = {
	#JAP_china_step_up_war_effort = {
	#
	#	icon = jap_conquer_china
	#
	#	available = {
	#		JAP_has_idea_JAP_intervene_in_china = yes
	#	}
	#
	#	visible = {
	#		JAP_has_idea_JAP_intervene_in_china = yes
	#		any_enemy_country = {
	#			is_literally_china = yes
	#		}
	#	}
	#
	#	fire_only_once = no
	#
	#	ai_will_do = {
	#		factor = 50
	#	}
	#	modifier = {
	#
	#	}
	#
	#	days_remove = 90
	#	days_re_enable = 0
	#
	#	cost = 25
	#
	#	complete_effect = {
	#		JAP_intervene_in_china_level_down = yes
	#	}
	#}
	JAP_ichi_go = {
		icon = jap_conquer_china
		available = {
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				has_capitulated = no
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_tojos_cabinet
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_literally_china = yes
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				NOT = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				date < 1944.1.1
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					USA = {
						has_war = no
					}
				}
				USA = {
					add_war_support = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					threat < 0.5
				}
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 15
					name = JAP_exploit_china
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 5
					name = JAP_exploit_china
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = JAP_ichi_go
				days = 360
			}
			activate_mission_tooltip = JAP_conquer_china
			set_country_flag = JAP_conquer_china_activate
		}
	}
	JAP_conquer_china = {
		icon = jap_conquer_china
		available = {
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				OR = {
					has_capitulated = yes
					exists = no
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			JAP_has_idea_JAP_intervene_in_china = yes
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_literally_china = yes
			}
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = JAP_conquer_china_activate
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 360
		timeout_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.15
		}
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.03
			add_war_support = 0.07
		}
	}
}

			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = ENG
					ENG = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				ENG = {
					country_event = {
						id = jap_armor.801
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				USA = {
					country_event = {
						id = jap_armor.801
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				MON = {
					transfer_state = 952
				}
				MON = {
					transfer_state = 954
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					761 = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					952 = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
				}

				}
				MON = {
					transfer_state = 952
